df6 = part[(part['SIZE'] <= 9) | (part['BRAND'] == 'Brand#35') & (part['P_NAME'] != 'l')]
df7 = df5.merge(df6, left_on='PS_PARTKEY', right_on='P_PARTKEY')
df8 = lineitem.merge(df7, left_on='L_SUPPKEY', right_on='PS_SUPPKEY')
df9 = orders[(orders['CLERK'] != 'C') | (orders['O_COMMENT'] != 'l') | (orders['O_COMMENT'] != 'e') | (orders['ORDERPRIORITY'] == '5-LOW') | (orders['ORDERPRIORITY'].isin(['5-LOW', '3-MEDIUM', '4-NOT SPECIFIED', '2-HIGH'])) & (orders['O_COMMENT'] == 'o') | (orders['O_CUSTKEY'] != 84894) | (orders['O_COMMENT'] == '.') | (orders['O_ORDERKEY'] == 389)]
df10 = df9[['ORDERSTATUS', 'ORDERDATE', 'O_COMMENT', 'O_CUSTKEY', 'O_ORDERKEY', 'CLERK', 'TOTALPRICE']]
df11 = nation[(nation['N_NAME'].str.startswith('B')) | (nation['N_NAME'].str.startswith('V')) & (nation['N_NATIONKEY'] != 2)]
df12 = df11[['N_NATIONKEY', 'N_NAME', 'N_COMMENT']]
df13 = customer.merge(df12, left_on='C_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df14 = df10.merge(df13, left_on='O_CUSTKEY', right_on='C_CUSTKEY')
df15 = df8.merge(df14, left_on='L_ORDERKEY', right_on='O_ORDERKEY')
df16 = df15.groupby(by=['P_PARTKEY', 'ORDERDATE', 'MKTSEGMENT']).agg('sum', numeric_only=True)

df1 = lineitem[(lineitem['L_PARTKEY'] >= 145938) | (lineitem['L_ORDERKEY'] > 13) | (lineitem['TAX'] != 0.0035834698252595575) & (lineitem['SHIPDATE'] > '1992-04-27') | (lineitem['COMMITDATE'] <= '1998-10-16') & (lineitem['QUANTITY'] < 46) & (lineitem['L_ORDERKEY'] < 167) & (lineitem['SHIPMODE'].isin(['SHIP', 'MAIL', 'TRUCK', 'FOB', 'RAIL', 'REG AIR', 'AIR'])) | (lineitem['L_COMMENT'].str.startswith('s. '))]
df2 = part[['MFGR', 'P_NAME', 'SIZE', 'PT_COMMENT', 'P_PARTKEY', 'CONTAINER', 'TYPE', 'BRAND']]
df3 = partsupp.merge(df2, left_on='PS_PARTKEY', right_on='P_PARTKEY')
df4 = supplier[['S_COMMENT', 'S_ACCTBAL', 'S_NATIONKEY', 'S_SUPPKEY', 'S_ADDRESS']]
df5 = nation[(nation['N_COMMENT'].str.startswith('i')) | (nation['N_REGIONKEY'] <= 2)]
df6 = df4.merge(df5, left_on='S_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df7 = df3.merge(df6, left_on='PS_SUPPKEY', right_on='S_SUPPKEY')
df8 = df1.merge(df7, left_on='L_PARTKEY', right_on='PS_PARTKEY')
df9 = orders[['SHIPPRIORITY', 'ORDERSTATUS', 'O_COMMENT', 'CLERK', 'ORDERPRIORITY', 'ORDERDATE', 'O_ORDERKEY', 'O_CUSTKEY', 'TOTALPRICE']]
df10 = customer[(customer['C_PHONE'].str.startswith('18-')) & (customer['MKTSEGMENT'].isin(['FURNITURE'])) | (customer['MKTSEGMENT'] != 'MACHINERY') | (customer['C_ACCTBAL'] < 6626.88256403595) & (customer['C_COMMENT'] != 'a') | (customer['C_COMMENT'].str.startswith(' ')) | (customer['C_ACCTBAL'] <= 5067.844810819265)]
df11 = nation[['N_REGIONKEY', 'N_NAME', 'N_NATIONKEY']]
df12 = df10.merge(df11, left_on='C_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df13 = df9.merge(df12, left_on='O_CUSTKEY', right_on='C_CUSTKEY')
df14 = df8.merge(df13, left_on='L_ORDERKEY', right_on='O_ORDERKEY')
df15 = df14.groupby(by=['S_COMMENT', 'N_COMMENT', 'TOTALPRICE', 'P_PARTKEY']).agg('count')
